# Project Files

- c:\Users\USER\OneDrive\.cursor\scripts\windows_scan.ps1
- c:\Users\USER\OneDrive\.cursor\CONTRIBUTING.md

## c:\Users\USER\OneDrive\.cursor\scripts\windows_scan.ps1
```
<#
Windows network discovery script (PowerShell)
- Uses Test-Connection and Get-NetNeighbor to discover hosts
- Outputs JSON to ./artifacts/scan-<timestamp>.json
- Follow code style: try-catch, Write-Host colors
#>

param(
  [string] $Subnet = "192.168.1.0/24",
  [string] $OutDir = ".\artifacts"
)

try {
  if (-not (Test-Path -Path $OutDir)) {
    New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $OutDir | Out-Null
  }

  $timestamp = (Get-Date -Format "yyyyMMdd-HHmmss")
  $outfile = Join-Path $OutDir "scan-$timestamp.json"

  Write-Host "[INFO] Starting discovery for subnet $Subnet" -ForegroundColor Cyan

  # Ping sweep (convert /24 to list of addresses - lightweight)
  $ips = 1..254 | ForEach-Object { ($Subnet -replace "/24","").TrimEnd(".0") + "." + $_ }
  $results = @()

  foreach ($ip in $ips) {
    try {
      if (Test-Connection -ComputerName $ip -Count 1 -Quiet -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue) {
        # Attempt to resolve DNS name
        $host = try { [System.Net.Dns]::GetHostEntry($ip).HostName } catch { "" }
        # Get ARP entry (if populated)
        $arp = Get-NetNeighbor -AddressFamily IPv4 | Where-Object { $_.IPAddress -eq $ip } | Select-Object -First 1
        $mac = if ($arp) { $arp.LinkLayerAddress } else { "" }

        $obj = [pscustomobject]@{
          ip = $ip
          hostname = $host
          mac = $mac
          first_seen = (Get-Date).ToString("o")
        }
        $results += $obj
        Write-Host "[OK] $ip ($host) $mac" -ForegroundColor Green
      }
    } catch {
      Write-Host "[WARNING] scanning $ip failed: $_" -ForegroundColor Yellow
    }
  }

  # Save results
  $results | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 4 | Out-File -FilePath $outfile -Encoding utf8
  Write-Host "[INFO] Scan complete. Results saved to $outfile" -ForegroundColor Cyan
} catch {
  Write-Host "[ERROR] Discovery failed: $_" -ForegroundColor Red
  exit 1
}

```

## c:\Users\USER\OneDrive\.cursor\CONTRIBUTING.md
```
# Contributing Guidelines

## Security & Privacy

### Network Scanning
- **Only scan networks you own or have explicit written authorization to scan**
- Never commit scan results or network topology data to the repository
- All scan artifacts are excluded via `.gitignore` - do not override this
- Use GitHub Actions artifacts or private storage (GCS) for scan outputs

### Credentials & Secrets
- **Never commit API keys, passwords, or service account keys**
- Use GitHub Secrets for CI/CD workflows
- For local development, use environment variables or system credential stores
- Review `.gitignore` before committing to ensure sensitive files are excluded

## Code Style

### PowerShell Scripts
- Use try-catch blocks for error handling
- Use Write-Host with color coding: Cyan for info, Green for success, Yellow for warnings, Red for errors
- Include parameter validation
- Add comments explaining network operations

### Python Scripts
- Follow PEP 8 style guidelines
- Include docstrings for functions and modules
- Use type hints where appropriate
- Handle exceptions gracefully with informative error messages

## Pull Request Process

1. **Test locally first**: Run scripts and demos in your environment before submitting PRs
2. **Update documentation**: If adding features, update relevant docs in `docs/`
3. **Check security**: Ensure no sensitive data is included
4. **Run linters**: Fix any linting errors before submitting
5. **Update CHANGELOG**: Document significant changes (if applicable)

## Running Scans

### Before Running Network Scans
- Verify you have authorization to scan the target network
- Understand the impact of your scan (avoid aggressive scanning on production networks)
- Use appropriate scan intensity (start with ping scans, escalate only if needed)

### Handling Scan Results
- Store results in `artifacts/` directory (gitignored)
- Do not commit scan results to the repository
- Use GitHub Actions artifacts for CI/CD scan outputs
- For sensitive networks, use private storage (GCS bucket with restricted access)

## AI/ML Demos

- Keep demos educational and well-documented
- Include requirements.txt with version pins where possible
- Add Jupyter notebooks for interactive exploration
- Document assumptions and limitations

## Questions?

Open an issue for questions about:
- Network scanning best practices
- Security concerns
- Code style questions
- Feature requests

```
